"Located in Huoying Subdistrict, Changping District, Beijing, the Shoukai Long Street offers a comprehensive range of dining, entertainment, and lodging services. With a total length of approximately 650 meters, a total construction area of 154,000 square meters, and a business area of 94,000 square meters, it consists of three parts: the South District, the North District, and a central shared garden. It is scheduled to open in June 2023. The Shoukai Long Street boasts a rich array of night-time and day-time economic activities. It is a demonstration project for ""Night Economy 3.0."" On the evening of June 28, 2025, a series of night-time economic activities in Changping District kicked off here. In collaboration with film and television cultural IPs, the event recreated a Tang Dynasty scene, featuring performances such as the Imperial Concubine's Parade and the Feather Dance. The Chang'an Night Market hosted over 30 themed banquets, boosting the restaurant industry's turnover rate by 3.2 times. The street boasts numerous major brands, including Huifengtang, Pizza Hut, Starbucks, and KFC in the dining sector; Huawei, Xiaomi, Nike, Li Ning, and Anta in the shopping sector; Perfect World Cinema and Mei KTV in the entertainment sector; and Tong Ren Tang and Jia Jia Yue Supermarket in the lifestyle sector. However, the street lacks sufficient publicity. Many residents of the six urban districts know Changping for its Ming Tombs, Juyongguan Pass, and Xinzhuang, but are unaware of Long Street."

"I loved this shopping street the first time I visited! The open-air design is much more interesting than those boxy indoor malls. It's a bit far from the subway, though, which is why I'd overlooked this gem. The entire outdoor mall is designed like a city block, with many independent buildings on either side, each four stories high. The ground floor is typically occupied by fast food, while the upper floors are for shopping, a gym, and more. At first glance, the signs aren't very obvious, but upon closer inspection, I discovered there are quite a few shops, offering a wide variety, many catering to a young demographic. The center is designed like a garden, which can also be used for temporary exhibitions. When I visited, the Chang'an Lychee Exhibition was underway, and the decorations were very charming. Each building has elevators and escalators, and the amenities are very comprehensive. In the summer, when the weather gets quite hot, there are water mist cooling devices on the ceiling, which create a magical atmosphere. Because of the heat, the open-air area was sparsely populated, and I thought it wasn't popular. But once I got to the shops and North Street, I realized how crowded it was. On weekends, many people from nearby bring their children here for playtime or tutoring. During lunch time, every store is filled with parents with children, enjoying the weekend together."

"The project's rigid division into two blocks, with buildings 50 meters apart, posed a significant challenge. How could the two blocks be connected? The introduction of a pedestrian skywalk was imperative. Two newly constructed skywalks create new open spaces in the air, offering different perspectives on the building. Visitors can walk on the bridges or lean on the railings to admire the scenery, becoming part of the scenery for others. Much like the Qingming Festival painting Along the River, the project creates a storytelling, layered commercial landscape. Traditional commercial streets are linear, with customers walking from one end to the other. As commerce flourished, it expanded across a flat surface. In the design of LONG Street, this horizontal flow is continued on the facade, with outdoor staircases creating a three-dimensional commercial street where visitors can ""fly over the eaves and walls."" Pedestrians, following their interests, explore the area, easily climbing to higher levels. This enhances the popularity of the upper commercial areas and creates a scene of life like a ""street market in the sky."" The new commercial street should reflect Chinese culture, as the Chinese national character is implicit and graceful. The design cloaks the existing building in a translucent ""coat""a wood-colored ""grille"" cladding, a design language extracted from ancient architectural components. The ""grille"" creates a visual and spatial effect of separation yet continuity, adding a hazy, graceful beauty and a touch of literati elegance to the building."
"Shoukai Long Street is quite different and innovative from the average mall, but compared to other traditional malls, it's not very crowded on weekends. I'm not sure if it's the heat or if there's something wrong with the mall's operations. Perhaps all malls share the same fate: bustling initially but then fade away. I hope Shoukai Long Street can persevere!"
"Occasionally, I'm captivated by the designers' ingenuity when I pass by. The streamlined 3D design extends to the facade, creating a three-dimensional commercial street with outdoor staircases that allow for ""flying over eaves and walls."" I can follow my interests, exploring up and down, imagining a life in this ""street market in the sky."" The ground floor is a perfect spot for taking the kids out for a date, and when there's a large outdoor performance or trendy market, the adjacent food stalls offer a wonderful place to enjoy a meal while listening to music."

"This is considered a new commercial landmark in the Huilongguan area, with over 800,000 high-quality consumers within a 5-kilometer radius. It fills a commercial void at the junction of Huilongguan and Tiantongyuan. Last year, a pedestrian shopping street opened near my Huilongguan residential complex. It's transformed from a wasteland into a vibrantly lit space, upgraded from the original residential amenities to a block-style, open-plan consumer space. I've watched it being built bit by bit, but never visited. This time, on a whim, I decided to bring my kids for a stroll. Located on Huoying Street in the central Huitian District of Changping, the Shoukai Long Street differs from traditional box-shaped shopping malls in that it's an open-plan street dotted with greenery, creating an organic fusion of nature and commerce. Merchants are located in multi-story spaces on both sides of the street, and art-themed basketball courts, children's playgrounds, coffee carts, and art installations are scattered throughout the street, adding vitality to the city's public spaces. The commercial street is about 650 meters long. It is the first full-time quality life commercial pedestrian street in northern Beijing carefully built by the Changping District Government. Adhering to the concept of ""revitalizing the youthful power of the upper city"", it is positioned as the ""city enjoyment life center"". It is a new living space consisting of three parts: business, office and central shared garden on the northern extension of the central axis. The commercial section in the south area creates a quality life block, and the industrial section in the north area creates a smart Internet of Things future industrial community. The landscape lighting of the commercial area is well done at night, and you can feel the full vitality and fashion. The surrounding residents come here to shop. At night, the block will be transformed into a free and relaxing ""city that never sleeps"". Surrounding residents can beat the heat, enjoy the cool air, enjoy midnight snacks, and feel the vitality of the night economy."

"The first LONG Street is a shining pearl of northern Beijing's commerce. The open block design cleverly integrates nature and commerce, covering trendy retail, parent-child entertainment and other business formats, and is equipped with four theme spaces and immersive cultural activities. It not only makes up for the shortcomings of regional consumption, but also reshapes the vitality of the Huitian area with the concept of ""urban oasis"", which can be regarded as a model of urban renewal."
"Over the past two years, there have been sporadic street openings catering to the leisure and entertainment needs of Huilongguan residents. The central shopping mall area has hosted a variety of events, both large and small. Huilongguan's first street, also known as Shoukai LONG Street, is located at the intersection of Huilongguan East Street and Huoying West Road. With a total construction area of 154,000 square meters, it consists of two districts, north and south. The specific layout is as follows: The South District: This commercial district focuses on lifestyle, dining, entertainment, and innovative business formats, creating new consumer spaces. The district is divided into three themed spaces. The southern end, ""Huilongji,"" showcases the city's trendy lifestyle and features Changping District's first ultra-stunning panoramic naked-eye 3D screen. The central ""Huanhuo Plaza"" offers a themed space integrating leisure, art, technology, and culture. The northern end, ""Magnetic Plaza,"" houses Changping District's first comprehensive sports plaza. North District: Designed as an industrial office area, it aims to create a ""garden-style technology and smart valley"" and create an urban living room. Through office and commercial facilities, it meets the work and social needs of office workers. Central Shared Garden: Utilizing nearly one-fifth of the area, the ""Central Shared Garden"" integrates natural greenery into modern architecture. Collaborating with trendsetting artists to create Beijing's first art oasis, this district, combined with diverse and dynamic artistic IPs and popular check-in spots, creates a high-quality lifestyle district that blends nature and art."

"Shoukai Long Street in Changping, Beijing, is a comprehensive commercial district integrating shopping, leisure, entertainment, and dining. It boasts numerous dining options, including Lelecha and LAVAZZA, which offer specialty drinks, as well as specialty brands like Xingju Zai Sanbei, catering to diverse consumer preferences. Furthermore, Shoukai Long Street serves as the Huitian District's first night economy themed district. From June 28 to August 2025, Changping District will be hosting a series of night economy events centered around it. During this period, the pedestrian street will be adorned with lights and the ""Li Ye Chang'an Banquet"" themed cultural event, incorporating film and television cultural IP. Numerous shops will recreate the bustling streets of Chang'an during the Tang Dynasty, while a variety of activities will be held, including a grand fashion show and a variety of magic tricks from the Fangshi Market. This will provide an immersive cultural experience, allowing consumers to enjoy shopping and dining while immersing themselves in the unique cultural atmosphere."

"Shoukai Long Street is an urban renewal project in Beijing's Changping District, aiming to create a lifestyle center integrating commerce, dining, entertainment, and sports. Located in Huoying Subdistrict in Changping District's Huitian District, the project has a total construction area of approximately 154,000 square meters, including approximately 60,000 square meters of above-ground commercial space in the first phase and approximately 40,000 square meters in the second phase industrial park. The pedestrian street, approximately 650 meters long, features a design that draws pedestrians upward, creating a rich, layered commercial landscape. The opening of Shoukai Long Street not only provides local residents with a new shopping and entertainment venue, but also revitalizes the area by revitalizing inefficient existing buildings and providing new ideas for the revitalized and utilized commercial and office space throughout the city. Furthermore, the opening of Shoukai Long Street demonstrates Shoukai Group's proactive exploration and practice in urban renewal. By renovating and upgrading existing buildings, it provides a modern commercial space and injects new impetus into the region's economic and social development. This project not only meets the daily needs of residents but also enhances their quality of life, becoming the first high-quality lifestyle commercial pedestrian street in northern Beijing."

"Main Title: Shoukai Long Street, Creating a New Urban Lifestyle. Commercial streets have long played a crucial role in urban development. Today, with the continuous advancement of urbanization, people's expectations of commercial streets are gradually changing. As a key project of Shoukai Group, Shoukai Long Street has emerged as a result. More than just a shopping mall, it embodies a new urban lifestyle. 1. An Indoor Space for All Seasons. Located in the heart of the capital, Shoukai Long Street offers convenient transportation and comprehensive amenities. The interior design concept is also unique, incorporating the beauty of each season into the interior space. In spring, long waterfalls and lush greenery create a sense of being immersed in nature. In summer, spacious corridors and a cool atmosphere offer a respite from the stifling heat of the outdoors. In autumn, colorful decorations and falling leaves create a warm atmosphere. In winter, warm lights and piping hot beverages create a festive atmosphere. 2. Diverse Shopping Experience: Shoukai Long Street boasts a diverse shopping experience, encompassing everything from global fashion brands to local designers, from daily necessities to high-end luxury goods. Here, visitors can enjoy the joy of shopping while experiencing the collision and fusion of different cultures. Furthermore, Shoukai Long Street offers a wide range of entertainment options, such as a cinema, karaoke, a children's playground, and a sports center, catering to the needs of diverse demographics. 3. Unique Experiences in a Culinary Capital: Shoukai Long Street offers a diverse selection of culinary delights from around the world, from classic Chinese and Western cuisine to exotic specialties. Not only can this place satisfy your taste buds, but it can also offer a sense of interaction and exchange between different cultures. Furthermore, Shoukai Long Street offers a variety of culinary experiences, such as cooking classes and wine tastings, allowing visitors to immerse themselves in delicious food and experience the beauty of life. In conclusion: Shoukai Long Street is more than just a shopping mall; it embodies a new urban lifestyle. Its unique design, diverse shopping experiences, and cultural exchange have captivated numerous urbanites. In the future, Shoukai Long Street will continue to leverage its core advantages to provide urban residents with a richer and more diverse life experience, becoming an important driving force for urban development."
